		function tryloginout(loginPrefix, redirectUrl) {
			// TCAP-4261: redirectUrl = currentUrl, 靜態化首頁的currentUrl會變成有加?previewHost=[首頁]，所以改用window.location.href
			if (typeof redirectUrl === "undefined" || redirectUrl == '') redirectUrl = window.location.href;
			var loginUrl = loginPrefix + encodeURIComponent(redirectUrl)+"&locale=en".replace("-","_");
			var cookieData = 'org.springframework.web.servlet.i18n.CookieLocaleResolver.LOCALE=' + "en".replace("-", "_") + ';path=/;domain=' + getSubdomain();
			document.cookie = cookieData;
			//if(window.console) console.log("loginUrl:"+loginUrl);
			//if(window.console) console.log("cookieData:"+cookieData);
			window.location.href = loginUrl;
		}

		function getSubdomain() {
			if (location.hostname.endsWith("develop.ttsev.idv.tw")){return "sso.develop.ttsev.idv.tw"}
			else if (location.hostname === "localhost"){return "sso.develop.ttsev.idv.tw"}
			else if (location.hostname.endsWith("ttsev.idv.tw")){return "sso.ttsev.idv.tw"}
			else return "security.taiwantrade.com";
			/*
			var parts = location.hostname.split('.');
			var subdomain = parts.shift();
			var upperleveldomain = parts.join('.');
			var sndleveldomain = parts.slice(-2).join('.');
			//if(window.console) console.log("parts:"+parts.length);
			//if(window.console) console.log("subdomain:"+subdomain);
			//if(window.console) console.log("upperleveldomain:"+upperleveldomain);
			//if(window.console) console.log("sndleveldomain:"+sndleveldomain);
			return upperleveldomain;
			*/
		}

			function isMobileDevice() {
				if (/Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
					return true;
				} else {
					return false;
				}
			}

			try {
				methods.push(headerItemMethod);
			} catch (e) {
			}
			function headerItemMethod() {
				$(document).ready(function() {
					if (isMobileDevice()) {
						$('.TopBar .TopNav .navItemBlk .Item.service').click(function() {
							var check = $(this).find('ul').attr('style');
							if (typeof(check)  === "undefined") {
								$(this).find('ul').attr('style', 'display: block; padding: 0px 0;');
								$(this).find('span').css('backgroundPosition', '-5px -968px');
							} else {
								if (check == 'display: block; padding: 0px 0;') {
									$(this).find('ul').attr('style', 'display: none;');
									$(this).find('span').css('backgroundPosition', '-5px -8px');
								} else {
									$(this).find('ul').attr('style', 'display: block; padding: 0px 0;');
									$(this).find('span').css('backgroundPosition', '-5px -968px');
								}
							}
						});
					}
				});
			}

		methods.push(searchBarMethod1);
		function searchBarMethod1() {
			var originalWidth = $("#searchWord").outerWidth();

			$('.stPrd > ul > li').click(function (e) {
				var _this = e.currentTarget;
				var _text = $(_this).html();
				var selectItem = document.getElementById("selectItem");
				selectItem.innerHTML = _text;
				$(selectItem).attr('type', $(_this).attr('data-type'));
				try {
					$('#mainSearchFrom #type').val($(selectItem).attr('type'));
				} catch (err) {
				}

				var windowsWidth = $(window).width();
				if (windowsWidth > 768) {
				} else {
					var ww1 = $(selectItem).outerWidth();
					var maxWidth = 40 + originalWidth - ww1;
					$("#searchWord").attr('style', 'width:' + (40 + originalWidth - ww1) + 'px;');
				}
			});

			var selectItem = document.getElementById("selectItem");
			var type = $('#mainSearchFrom #type');
			var style = $('#mainSearchFrom #style');
			//只有Product Search才會改變預設的下拉
			if (type.val() == 'supplier' || type.val() == 'company') {
				selectItem.innerHTML = 'Supplier';
				$(selectItem).attr('type', 'supplier');
			} else if (type.val() == 'product') {
				if (style.val() == 'supplier') {
					selectItem.innerHTML = 'Supplier';
					$(selectItem).attr('type', 'supplier');
				} else {
					selectItem.innerHTML = 'Product';
					$(selectItem).attr('type', 'product');
				}
			} else if (type.val() == 'post') {
				selectItem.innerHTML = 'Trading Post';
				$(selectItem).attr('type', 'post');
			} else  {
				//包含 if (type.val() == '') 
				
						selectItem.innerHTML = 'Product';
						$(selectItem).attr('type', 'product');
								
			
			}

			$("#searchWord").keyup(function(event) {
				if (event.keyCode == 13) {
					doWordSubmit();
				}
			});
		}

		function doWordSubmitWithParam(word) {
			var searchWord = document.getElementById("searchWord");
			searchWord.value = word;
			doWordSubmit();
		}

		function doWordSubmitWithParamAndSubword(word, subword, type) {
			clearForm();
			$('#mainSearchFrom #word').val(word);
			$('#mainSearchFrom #subword').val(subword);
			$('#mainSearchFrom #type').val(type);
			get_action();
		}

		function doWordSubmit() {
		    var baseTarget = $('#btarget').attr('target'); 
			if(window.console) console.log('baseTarget:'+baseTarget);
			if(baseTarget === undefined) baseTarget = '_self';
			if(window.console) console.log('baseTarget:'+baseTarget);
			var searchWord = document.getElementById("searchWord").value;
			var selectItem = document.getElementById("selectItem");
			var $selectItem = $(selectItem);
			if(window.console) console.log('selectItem type:'+$selectItem.attr('type'));
			if (searchWord == '') {
				// alert('Please Input Query Word');
			} else if (searchWord == '*') {
				 clearForm();
				 $('#mainSearchFrom #word').val('*');
				 get_action();
			} else {
				if ($selectItem.attr('type') == 'sample') {
					get_actionSample();
				} else {
					var type = $('#mainSearchFrom #type');
					if ($selectItem.attr('type') == 'product') {
						link = '/products/search/' + encodeURIComponent(searchWord) + '-gallery.html';
						window.open(link, baseTarget);
					} else if ($selectItem.attr('type') == 'supplier') {
						link = '/products/search/' + encodeURIComponent(searchWord) + '-supplier.html';
						window.open(link, baseTarget);
					} else if ($selectItem.attr('type') == 'post') {
						link = '/tradepost/search/' + encodeURIComponent(searchWord);
						window.open(link, baseTarget);
					}
				}
			}
		}

		function get_action() {
			var form = $('#mainSearchFrom');
			var type = $('#mainSearchFrom #type').val();
			// if (window.console) console.log('get action:' + type);
			if (type == 'event') {
				form.attr("action", "/events/search");
				//document.form.action = '/events/search';
			} else if (type == 'product') {
				form.attr("action", "/products/search");
			} else if (type == 'supplier') {
				form.attr("action", "/products/search");
			} else if (type == 'post') {
				form.attr("action", "/tradepost/search");
				var post_company = $('#mainSearchFrom #post_company').val();
				if(post_company !='' ) form.attr("action", "/tradepost/company/"+post_company);
				$('#mainSearchFrom #post_company').val('');
			} else if (type == 'news') {
				form.attr("action", "/tradenews/search");
			} else if (type == 'company') {
				form.attr("action", "/suppliers/search");
			} else if (type == 'sample') {
				var url = 'http://www.idealez.com/product-search/' + toEZLangCode($('#mainSearchFrom #lang').val()) + '/' + $('#mainSearchFrom #word').val();
				// if (window.console) console.log($('#mainSearchFrom #word').val() + 'to ez:'+url);
				window.open(url,'_blank');
				return;
			} else{
				alert("Please Choose a legal search type");
			}
			// if (window.console) console.log('get action: form:'+form.attr("id")+':'+form.attr("method")+':'+form.attr("action"));
			// form.submit();
			cleanEmptyParamAndSubmit();
		}

		function get_actionSample() {

		function get_actionList() {
			var form = $('#mainSearchFrom');
			var type = $('#mainSearchFrom #type').val();

			if (type == 'event') {
				form.attr("action", "/events/list");
			} else if (type == 'product') {
				form.attr("action", "/products/list");
			} else if (type == 'supplier') {
				form.attr("action", "/products/list");
			} else if (type == 'post') {
				form.attr("action", "/tradepost/list");
			} else if (type == 'news') {
				form.attr("action", "/tradenews/list");
			} else if (type == 'company') {
				form.attr("action", "/suppliers/list");
			} else {
				alert("Please Choose a legal search type");
			}
			// form.submit();
			cleanEmptyParamAndSubmit();
		}

		function toEZLangCode(languageId) {
			if (languageId != '') {
				if (languageId == '43') return "ja_JP";
				else if (languageId == '44') return "zh_CN";
				else if (languageId == '41') return "zh_TW";
			}
			return "en_US";
		}

		function gotoProductListForTaitraAdv(taitracode, cname) {
			var windowsWidth = $(window).width();

			var menu_select = document.getElementById("menu_select");
			var menu_select_val = document.getElementById("menu_select").value;

			if (windowsWidth > 768) {
			} else {
				if (menu_select_val != "") {
					try {
						var temp = document.getElementById("menuDiv_" + menu_select_val);
						temp.style.display = "none";
					} catch (err) {
					}
				}
			}

			if (windowsWidth > 768) {
				gotoProductListForTaitra(taitracode);
			} else {
				if (cname == "navItem") {
					if (taitracode == menu_select_val) {
						gotoProductListForTaitra(taitracode);
					} else {
						menu_select.value = taitracode;
						try {
							var temp = document.getElementById("menuDiv_" + taitracode);
							temp.style.display = "block";
						} catch (err) {
						}
					}
				} else {
					gotoProductListForTaitra(taitracode);
				} 
			}
		}

		function showLightPic(pid, favorited, pName, pUrl, picUrl) {

			javascript:parent.jQuery.fancybox.open({href:openUrl, type:'ajax', width:"380px", height:"auto", autoSize:false, closeBtn:false});
		}

		function cleanEmptyParamAndSubmit() {
			var form = $('#mainSearchFrom');
			var style = $('#mainSearchFrom #style').val();
			var type = $('#mainSearchFrom #type').val();
			var searchWord = document.getElementById("searchWord").value;

			if (type == 'event') {
				setCookie('searchWord_event', searchWord);
			} else if (type == 'product') {
				setCookie('searchWord_product', searchWord);
			} else if (type == 'supplier') {
				setCookie('searchWord_product', searchWord);
			} else if (type == 'post') {
				setCookie('searchWord_post', searchWord);
			} else if (type == 'news') {
				setCookie('searchWord_news', searchWord);
			} else if (type == 'company') {
				setCookie('searchWord_company', searchWord);
			}

			var myForm = document.getElementById('mainSearchFrom');
			var allInputs = myForm.getElementsByTagName('input');

			var input, i;
			for (i = 0; input = allInputs[i]; i++) {
				if (input.getAttribute('name')) {
					var columnName = input.getAttribute('name');

					if (columnName == 'did' || columnName == 'lang' || columnName == 'menu_select') {
						input.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
						input.setAttribute('name', null);
					} else if (!input.value) {
						input.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
						input.setAttribute('name', null);
					} else if (columnName == 'page') {
						if (input.value == '1') {
							input.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
							input.setAttribute('name', null);
						}
					} else if (columnName == 'rows') {
						var style = $('#mainSearchFrom #style').val();
						//disabled rows for default value
						if (style == 'gallery') {
							if (input.value == '18') {
								input.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
								input.setAttribute('name', null);
							}
						} else {
							if (input.value == '20') {
								if (type == 'company' || type == 'post' || type == 'news' || type == 'event') {
								} else {
									input.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
									input.setAttribute('name', null);
								}
							} else if (input.value == '10' ) {
								if (type == 'company' || type == 'post' || type == 'news' || type == 'event') {
									input.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
									input.setAttribute('name', null);
								}
							}
						}
					} else if (columnName == 'mode') {
						if (input.value == '0') {
							input.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
							input.setAttribute('name', null);
						} else if (input.value == '-1') {
							if(type == 'company' || type == 'post' || type == 'news' || type == 'event'){
								input.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
								input.setAttribute('name', null);
							}
						}
					} else if (columnName == 'stateId') {
						if (type == 'company' || type == 'post' || type == 'news' || type == 'event'){
							input.setAttribute('disabled', 'disabled');
							input.setAttribute('name', null);
						}
					}
				}
			}

			var groupLength = $('#mainSearchFrom #group1').val().length + $('#mainSearchFrom #group2').val().length + 
							$('#mainSearchFrom #group3').val().length + $('#mainSearchFrom #group4').val().length + 
							$('#mainSearchFrom #group5').val().length + $('#mainSearchFrom #group0').val().length;
			// if (groupLength == 0)
			form.attr("method", "get");
			form.submit();
		}

		function setCookie(cname, cvalue) {
			var d = new Date();
			d.setTime(d.getTime() + (7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
			var expires = "expires=" + d.toUTCString();

			var myDate = new Date();
			var dataVal = '';
			dataVal += '' + myDate.getFullYear(); // year
			dataVal += '' + ('0' + (myDate.getMonth() + 1)).slice(-2); // month
			dataVal += '' + ('0' + myDate.getDate()).slice(-2) // date
			dataVal += '' + ('0' + myDate.getHours()).slice(-2); // hour
			dataVal += '' + ('0' + myDate.getMinutes()).slice(-2); // minute
			dataVal += '' + ('0' + myDate.getSeconds()).slice(-2); // second
			dataVal += cvalue;

			var idx = 0;
			var lastDate = '2199' + '12' + '31' + '23' + '59' + '59';
			for (var i = 1; i <= 10; i++) {
				var cookieColumn = getCookie(cname + '_' + i);
				if (cookieColumn.length == 0) {
					idx = i;
					break;
				} else {
					var ca = cookieColumn.substring(0, 14);
					var cv = cookieColumn.substring(14);

					if (cv == cvalue) {
						idx = i;
						break;
					}

					if (parseInt(lastDate) >= parseInt(ca)) {
						lastDate = ca;
						idx = i;
					}
				}
			}
			document.cookie = cname + '_' + idx + '=' + dataVal + '; ' + expires + ';path=/;domain=' + window.location.hostname;
		}

		function getCookie(cname) {
			var name = cname + "=";
			var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
			for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
				var c = ca[i];
				while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
				if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) {
					return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
				}
			}
			return "";
		}

		methods.push(logoMethod);
		function logoMethod() {
			var $wrapHeader = $('.Wrap .Header');
			var $siteLogo = $('#siteLogo');
			var $flashLogo, $largeLogo, $smallLogo, $newFlashLogo;
			if ($siteLogo.length > 0) {
				$flashLogo = $($siteLogo[0].children[0]).clone();
				$largeLogo = $($siteLogo[0].children[1]).clone();
				$smallLogo = $($siteLogo[0].children[2]).clone();
				$newFlashLogo = $($siteLogo[0].children[3]).clone();
			}

			/*
			 * PC: 有Flash先⽤用Flash
			 * 沒有Flash就⽤圖⽚一
			 *
			 * 如果沒有安裝 flash player，顯示圖片一
			 */
			var isMobileDevice = navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone/i) ||
							 navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) ||
							 navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i);
			if (swfobject.ua.pv && !isMobileDevice && $siteLogo.data('flash')) {
				var flashvars = {
					autostart: "true"
				};
				var params = {
					movie: "//file01.itaiwantrade.com/9e519b79-fac3-4f14-9de5-9d2ad67cf254/9c28f47b-0e2e-4f5d-8e63-d23b3c22a376[1].swf",
					allowfullscreen: "false",
					quality: "high",
					wmode: "transparent",
					menu: "false"
				};
				var attributes = {
					align: "middle"
				};
				swfobject.embedSWF($siteLogo.data('flash'), "logoFlash", "175", "70", "10.0.0", "", flashvars, params, attributes);

				if (typeof($newFlashLogo) != "undefined") {
					// $flashLogo.css('display', 'block');
					$('.Wrap .Header h1 div').append($newFlashLogo);
					$newFlashLogo.css('display', 'block');
				}
			} else {
				$('.Wrap .Header h1').empty();
				$('.Wrap .Header h1').append($largeLogo);
				if (typeof($largeLogo) != "undefined") {
					$largeLogo.css('display', 'block');
				}
			}

			if ($('div.TopBar div.site-logo').html() == '') {
	 			$('div.TopBar div.site-logo').hide();
	 		}

			if ($siteLogo.length > 0) {
				$siteLogo.remove();
			}
		}

               <div class="idx_LeftCol" id="show_left"><script type="text/javascript">
			function isMobileDevice() {
				if (/Android|webOS|iPhone|iPad|iPod|BlackBerry|IEMobile|Opera Mini/i.test(navigator.userAgent)) {
					return true;
				} else {
					return false;
				}
			}

			methods.push(menuMethod);
			function menuMethod() {
				$(document).ready(function() {
					if (isMobileDevice()) {
						$('.Content.categoryTopPage .topcontBlk .idx_LeftCol .nav li').each(function() {
							$(this).click(function() {
								var href = $(this).find('a').first().attr('href');
								if ($(this).find('a').first().attr('class') == 'navItem') {
									if (href.substring(0, 1) == '#') {
										var tempHref = $(this).find('a').first().attr('tempHref');
										$(this).find('a').first().attr('href', tempHref);
									} else {
										var hrefid = $(this).find('a').first().attr('id');
										try {
											$(this).find('a').first().attr('tempHref', href).attr('href', '#menuli_' + hrefid.substring(5));
										} catch(e) {
											$(this).find('a').first().attr('tempHref', href).attr('href', '#menuli_' + hrefid);
										}
									}
								}

								var $current = $(this);
								var $parent = $(this).parent();
								$parent.find('li .subMenu').attr('style', 'display: none;');
								$(this).find('.subMenu').first().attr('style', 'display: block;');
							});
						});
					}
				});
			}
		</script><ul class="nav">

			   	$('.slider-nav .slick-slide').eq(0).addClass('slick-active');

type="text/javascript">
			function open_close(id) {
				var o = document.getElementById(id);
				if (id == 'show_left') {
					var or = document.getElementById('show_right');
					if (or != null) {
						or.style.display = 'none';
					}
				}

				if (id == 'show_right') {
					var ol = document.getElementById('show_left');
					if (ol != null) {
						ol.style.display = 'none';
					}
				}

				if (o != null) {
					if (o.style.display == 'block') {
						o.style.display = 'none';
					} else {
						o.style.display = 'block';
					}
				}
			}
		</script><script type="text/javascript">
